BZA' BAR MI BYA'O, ,BLO GROS CHEN PO,

RNAM PA THAMS CAD DANG DUS THAMS CAD DU THABS KYIS GNANG BA THAMS
CAD KYANG BKAG GO ,BLO GROS CHEN


@460B PO; DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA DGRA BCOM PA YANG DAG PAR RDZOGS
PA'I SANGS RGYAS LA NI BZA' BAR BYA BA'ANG MED NA NYA'I SHA BZA'
BA LTA CI SMOS TE, GZHAN YANG BYED DU MI

'JUG GO ,THUGS RJE CHEN PO SNGON DU 'GRO BA'I PHYIR SEMS CAN
THAMS CAD BU GCIG PA DANG 'DRA BAR GZIGS TE, DE'I PHYIR BU'I SHA
BZA' BAR MI GNANG BA YIN NO, ,DE NAS

BCAD PA 'DI DAG GSUNGS SO, ,SNGON CHAD GNYEN BSHES BYAS PHYIR

PAS, ,SHA RNAMS DANG NI BTZONG DAG DANG, ,KE'U DANG BYIS KU LA
SOGS DANG, ,BAG MED SNA TSOGS 'GYUR BA'I

CHANG, ,RNAL 'BYOR PAS NI RTAG TU SPANG, ,'BRU MAR DAG KYANG
SPANG BYA STE, ,BU GA PHUG PA'I KHRI YANG SPANG, ,SROG CHAGS DAG
NI PHRA MO RNAMS, ,DE NA RAB TU 'JIGS PHYIR RO, ,

,RTOG PA LAS NI 'DOD CHAGS SKYE, ,DE YI PHYIR NA BZA' MI BYA,
,ZAS KYI DBANG GIS 'DOD CHAGS

SKYE; ;'DOD CHAGS KYIS NI SEMS RMONGS BYED, ,RMONGS PAS SRID PA'I

SEMS CAN GSOD, ,SHA YI PHYIR

DAG PA'I SHA YANG MED, ,RGYU MED LAS NI YOD MIN PAS, ,DE YI PHYIR
NA BZA' MI BYA, ,RNAL 'BYOR PA NI DE DAG GIS, ,DES NA THAMS CAD
SPANG BYAR BYA, ,PHYOGS
